Normalizes \'left arm\' to \'arms\'."""\n        key = "torso" # Default\n        if not target_part_name:\n            key = "torso"\n        elif "head" in target_part_name: key = "head"\n        elif "leg" in target_part_name: key = "legs"\n        elif "arm" in target_part_name: key = "arms"\n        \n        self.history[key] = self.history.get(key, 0) + 1\n\n    def get_adaptation_penalty(self, target_part_name):\n        """Returns a damage reduction multiplier (0.0 to 1.0)."""\n        total = sum(self.history.values())\n        if total < 5: return 1.0 # Not enough data yet\n\n        key = "torso"\n        if not target_part_name:\n            key = "torso"\n        elif "head" in target_part_name: key = "head"\n        elif "leg" in target_part_name: key = "legs"\n        elif "arm" in target_part_name: key = "arms"\n\n        ratio = self.history.get(key, 0) / total\n        \n        # If player targets this part > 40% of the time, monsters adapt\n        if ratio > 0.4:\n            return 0.5 # 50% damage reduction (Blocked!)\n        elif ratio > 0.25:\n            return 0.8 # 20% reduction (Glancing hit)\n        \n        return 1.0 # Full damage\n\n    def save(self):\n        if not os.path.exists(os.path.dirname(self.filepath)):\n            os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(self.filepath))\n        with open(self.filepath, \'w\') as f:\n            json.dump(self.history, f)\n\n    def load(self):\n        if os.path.exists(self.filepath):\n            with open(self.filepath, \'r\') as f:\n                self.history = json.load(f)\n                \n    def get_boss_adaptation(self, target_part):\n        """Boss-level adaptation: 90% reduction if you are predictable."""\n        total = sum(self.history.values())\n        if total < 3: return 1.0\n        \n        ratio = self.history.get(target_part, 0) / total\n        if ratio > 0.3: # for k,v in d["parts"].items()}\n        return p\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- MONSTER CLASS ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Monster(Entity):\n    def __init__(self, key):\n        from data.monsters import MONSTER_TEMPLATES\n        t = MONSTER_TEMPLATES.get(key, {"name": "Glitch", "desc": "Error.", "type": MonsterType.ZOMBIE, "hp": 1, "dmg": MonsterType.ZOMBIE)\n        self.max_hp = t.get("hp", 10)\n        self.hp = self.max_hp\n        self.dmg = t.get("dmg", 1)\n        self.sanity_drain = t.get("drain", 0)\n        self.loot_keys = BehaviorState.DEAD\n            return True\n        self.behavior = BehaviorState.AGGRO\n        return False\n\n    def generate_loot(self):\n        items = []\n        for l_key in       if self.sanity < 20:\n            return "Wandering"\n        return "Stable"\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- CONTAINER & STRUCTURE ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Container(Entity):\n    def __init__(self, key_or_name, desc=None, locked=False):\n        name = key_or_name\n        description = desc if desc else "A container."\n        is_locked = locked\n\n        try:\n            from data.items import CONTAINER_TEMPLATES\n            if key_or_name in CONTAINER_TEMPLATES:\n                t =  pass \n\n        super().__init__(name)\n        self.description = description\n        self.locked = is_locked\n        self.inventory = []\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {\n            "name": self.name, \n            "desc": self.description, \n            "locked": self.locked, \n            "inv": [i.to_dict() for i in self.inventory], \n            "type": "CONTAINER"\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, d):\n        c = cls(d["name"], d["desc"], d["locked"])\n        c.inventory = [Item.from_dict(x) for x in d["inv"]]\n        return c\n\nclass Structure(Container):\n    def __init__(self, recipe_key):\n        from data.recipes import BUILDING_RECIPES\n        t = BUILDING_RECIPES.get(recipe_key, {"name": "Rubble", "desc": "Collapsed."})\n        super().__init__(t["name"], t.get("desc", ""), False)\n        self.recipe_key = recipe_key\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        d = super().to_dict()\n        d["type"] = "STRUCTURE"\n return s\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- LOCATION CLASS ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Location:\n    def __init__(self, name, description, location_id, x=0, y=0):\n        self.name = name\n        self.description = description\n        self.location_id = location_id\n        self.x = x\n        self.y = y\n        self.exits = {}\n        self.items = []\n        self.containers = []\n        self.structures = []\n        self.monsters = []\n        self.survivors = []\n        self.residents = []\n        # --- NEW STABILITY ATTRIBUTE ---\n        self.stability = 100 \n\n    def get_security_rating(self):\n        """Calculates how safe a room is based on barricades."""\n        defense = 0\n        for s in self.structures:\n            # Safely check for recipe_key without crashing on standard containers\n            if getattr(s, "recipe_key", None) == "barricade":\n                defense += 50 # Each barricade adds 50% safety\n        return min(defense, 100)\n\n    def update_stability(self, player_psychosis, has_fire):\n        """\n        Fire anchors reality. \n        Darkness + Psychosis causes the world to thin.\n        """\n        if has_fire:\n            # Fire restores stability quickly\n            self.stability = min(100, self.stability + 15)\n        elif player_psychosis > 50:\n            # Stability drops faster the more psychotic the player is\n            decay = 1 + (player_psychosis // 20)\n            self.stability -= decay\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {\n            "name": self.name, "desc": self.description, "id": self.location_id,\n            "x": self.x, "y": self.y, "exits": self.exits,\n            "items": [i.to_dict() for i in self.items],\n            "containers": [c.to_dict() for c in self.containers],\n            "structures": [s.to_dict() for s in self.structures],\n            "monsters": [m.to_dict() for m in self.monsters],\n            "survivors": [s.to_dict() for s in self.survivors]\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, d):\n        loc = cls(d["name"], d["desc"], d["id"], d.get("x", 0), d.get("y", 0))\n        loc.exits = d.get("exits", {})\n        loc.items = [Item.from_dict(i) for i in d.get("items", [])]\n        loc.containers = [Container.from_dict(c) for c in d.get("containers", [])]\n        loc.structures = [Structure.from_dict(s) for s in d.get("structures", [])]\n        loc.monsters = [Monster.from_dict(m) for m in d.get("monsters", [])]\n        loc.survivors = [Survivor.from_dict(s) for s in d.get("survivors", [])]\n        return loc\n        \nclass Campfire(Structure):\n    def __init__(self, recipe_key="campfire"):\n        super().__init__(recipe_key)\n        self.max_fuel = 2500\n        self.remaining_fuel = 2500\n        self.is_lit = True\n\n    def burn(self):\n        """Reduces fuel every turn."""\n        if self.is_lit:\n            self.remaining_fuel -= 1\n            if self.remaining_fuel <= 0:\n                self.is_lit = False\n                self.name = "Extinguished Campfire"\n--------\n# --- START OF FILE game_engine.py ---\n\nimport sys\nimport time\nimport random\nfrom world_manager import WorldManager\nfrom narrator import Narrator\nfrom entities import Item, Structure, BehaviorState, ItemType, Container, Campfire\nfrom parser import CommandParser\nfrom scent_tracking_system import ScentTrailManager, HunterAI\nfrom combat_pattern_recognition import CombatTacticsEngine\n\nclass GameEngine:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.wm = WorldManager()\n        self.parser = CommandParser()\n        self.scent_manager = ScentTrailManager()\n        self.tactics_engine = CombatTacticsEngine()\n        self.running = True\n        self.breach_active = False\n        self.breach_waves = 5\n        self.current_wave = 0\n\n    def start(self):\n        print("Initializing World...")\n        if not self.wm.load():\n            print("No save found. Generating new world...")\n            self.wm.create_new_world()\n        \n        # Load external systems\n        self.scent_manager.load()\n        self.tactics_engine.load()\n\n        print("\\n" + "="*50)\n        print("   S U R V I V A L   R P G")\n        print("   Commands: look, go [dir], take [item], i")\n        print("             attack [enemy] [head/legs/arms/torso]")\n        print("             recruit [survivor], search [corpse/container]")\n        print("             craft [item], build [struct]")\n        print("="*50 + "\\n")\n        \n        self.look()\n        self.loop()\n\n    def get_loc(self):\n        p = self.wm.player\n        return self.wm.generate_location(p.x, p.y)\n\n    def find_object_fuzzy(self, search_term, object_list):\n        if not search_term: return None\n        search_term = search_term.lower()\n        for obj in object_list:\n            if obj.name.lower() == search_term: return obj\n        for obj in object_list:\n            if search_term in obj.name.lower(): return obj\n        return None\n    \n    def tick_world(self):\n        p = self.wm.player\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n        \n        # --- 1. PHYSICAL DECAY ---\n        # Hunger increases by 0.15, Thirst by 0.25 per turn\n        p.hunger += 0.15\n        p.thirst += 0.25\n        \n        # Damage player if starving/dehydrated\n        if p.hunger >= 100 or p.thirst >= 100:\n            p.hp -= 1\n            if p.hunger >= 100: print("[!] You are starving.")\n            if p.thirst >= 100: print("[!] You are dying of thirst.")\n\n        # --- 2. FIRE & LIGHT DECAY ---\n        torch = p.equipment.get("off_hand")\n        is_lit_torch = torch and torch.props.get("fire")\n        \n        # Torch depletion\n        if is_lit_torch:\n            torch.props["lifespan"] -= 1\n            if torch.props["lifespan"] <= 0:\n                print("\\n[!] Your torch has flickered out.")\n                p.equipment["off_hand"] = None\n                p.fear += 20 # Panic from sudden darkness\n                is_lit_torch = False\n\n        # Campfire depletion\n        active_campfire = next((s for s in loc.structures if isinstance(s, Campfire) and s.is_lit), None)\n        if active_campfire:\n            active_campfire.burn() # Reduces 2500 fuel by 1\n\n        # --- 3. MENTAL STATE UPDATE ---\n        if active_campfire and active_campfire.is_lit:\n            p.update_mental_state(\'campfire\')\n        elif is_lit_torch:\n            p.update_mental_state(\'torch\')\n        else:\n            p.update_mental_state(None) # Applying darkness creep\n\n        if p.fear > 50:\n            # You are sweating/breathing heavy; monsters smell it.\n            self.scent_manager.add_scent(p.location_id) \n            \n        self.check_reality_shift()\n        p.clamp_stats()\n    \n\n    def check_reality_shift(self):\n        # Placeholder for reality shift logic\n        pass\n    def loop(self):\n        while self.running:\n            if self.wm.player.hp <= 0:\n                print("\\n\\n" + "#"*30 + "\\n    Y O U   H A V E   D I E D\\n" + "#"*30)\n                break\n            try:\n                cmd_raw = input("\\n> ").strip().lower()\n            except EOFError:\n                break\n            \n            parsed = self.parser.parse(cmd_raw)\n            if not parsed: continue\n            verb = parsed["verb"]\n            noun = parsed["noun"]\n            \n            turn_taken = self.process_command(verb, noun)\n            if turn_taken and self.running and not self.wm.player.is_dying:\n                self.monster_turns()\n                self.tick_world()\n                self.wm.player.update_status()\n            \n            if self.wm.player.psychosis >= 100:\n                print("\\n" + "!"*40)\n                print("YOUR MIND SNAPS. YOU LOSE CONTROL.")\n                print("!"*40)\n                forced_actions = ["go north", "go south", "attack torso", "drop all"]\n                cmd_raw = random.choice(forced_actions)\n                print(f"In a blur of terror, you {cmd_raw}...")\n                self.wm.player.psychosis -= 30\n                self.wm.player.fear += 20\n                # Process the forced command\n                parsed = self.parser.parse(cmd_raw)\n                if parsed:\n                    self.process_command(parsed["verb"], parsed["noun"])\n\n    def tick_breach(self):\n        loc = self.wm.get_location(0, 0) # The Safehouse\n        security = loc.get_security_rating()\n        \n        print(f"\\n--- BREACH WAVE {self.current_wave}/{self.breach_waves} ---")\n        print(f"Base Integrity: {security}%")\n\n        # 1. Residents provide defensive fire\n        for res in loc.residents:\n            if res.role == "Guard" and res.sanity > 20:\n                damage = random.randint(10, 20)\n                print(f"{res.name} fires from the barricades, dealing {damage} damage to the horde!")\n                # Logic to apply damage to the incoming wave\n        \n        # 2. Check for Structural Damage\n        if security < 100:\n            breach_chance = (100 - security) / 100\n            if random.random() < breach_chance:\n                print("A barricade splinters! The monsters are pushing through!")\n                # Reduce security or damage a random structure\n                target_struct = random.choice(loc.structures)\n                loc.structures.remove(target_struct)\n       \n        for res in loc.residents:\n            if res.sanity < 15:\n                print(f"\\n[!!!] {res.name} has snapped!")\n                print(f"{res.name} screams: \'THEY AREN\'T MONSTERS, THEY\'RE SAVIORS!\'")\n                print(f"{res.name} begins tearing down a barricade from the inside!")\n                # Immediate drop in security rating\n                loc.security_rating -= 30       \n\n    def end_breach(self, success):\n        if success:\n            print("\\n" + "="*60)\n            print("THE GREY RECENTES. THE SUN BREAKS THROUGH THE CLOUDS.")\n            print("The horde dissolves into ash. You have held the line.")\n            print("="*60)\n            self.wm.player.ground_reality() # Resets Psychosis to 0\n        else:\n            print("The safehouse has fallen. Reality dissolves into the void.")\n            self.running = False # Game Over\n\n    def process_command(self, verb, noun):\n        player = self.wm.player\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n\n        if player.is_dying:\n            allowed = ["use", "go", "inventory", "i", "quit"]\n            if verb not in allowed:\n                print("You are bleeding out! You can\'t do that right now!")\n                return False\n\n        if verb == "go":\n            dx, dy = 0, 0\n            if noun == "north": dy = 1\n            elif noun == "south": dy = -1\n            elif noun == "east": dx = 1\n            elif noun == "west": dx = -1\n            else:\n                print("Go where?")\n                return False\n            \n            player.x += dx\n            player.y += dy\n            new_loc = self.wm.generate_location(player.x, player.y)\n            player.location_id = new_loc.location_id\n            \n            # SCENT: Record movement\n            self.scent_manager.add_scent(player.location_id)\n            \n            print(f"You move {noun}...")\n            self.look()\n            return True\n\n        elif verb == "look": self.look(); return False \n        elif verb == "inventory" or verb == "i": player.print_inventory(); return False\n        elif verb == "status": self.cmd_status(); return False\n        elif verb == "take": return self.cmd_take(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "drop": return self.cmd_drop(noun, loc)\n        elif verb in ["open", "search"]: return self.cmd_open(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "use": return self.cmd_use(noun)\n        elif verb == "attack": return self.cmd_attack(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "build": return self.cmd_build(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "craft": return self.cmd_craft(noun)\n        elif verb == "recruit": return self.cmd_recruit(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "save": \n            self.wm.save()\n            self.scent_manager.save()\n            self.tactics_engine.save()\n            print("Game saved.")\n            return False\n        elif verb == "quit": self.running = False; return False\n        else: print(f"I don\'t know how to \'{verb}\'."); return False\n\n    def cmd_status(self):\n        p = self.wm.player\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n        print("\\n" + "═"*45)\n        print(" STATUS REPORT")\n        print("═"*45)\n        print(f" HP        : {p.hp}/100")\n        print(f" HUNGER    : {p.hunger:.1f}% {\'(STARVING!)\' if p.hunger > 80 else \'\'}")\n        print(f" THIRST    : {p.thirst:.1f}% {\'(DEHYDRATED!)\' if p.thirst > 80 else \'\'}")\n        print("-" * 45)\n        print(f" SANITY    : {p.sanity}%")\n        print(f" PSYCHOSIS : {p.psychosis}% {\'[REALITY FAILING]\' if p.psychosis > 70 else \'\'}")\n        print(f" FEAR      : {p.fear}% | PARANOIA  : {p.paranoia}%")\n        active_campfire = next((s for s in loc.structures if isinstance(s, Campfire) and s.is_lit), None)\n        torch = p.equipment.get("off_hand")\n        is_using_torch = torch and torch.props.get("fire")\n        print("-" * 45)\n        if active_campfire:\n            rate = 3 + (p.fire_timer // 5)\n            print(f" STATUS    : [GROUNDED] Sanctuary (Rate: -{rate}/turn)")\n            print(f" FIRE FUEL : {active_campfire.remaining_fuel}/2500 turns")\n        elif is_using_torch:\n            print(f" STATUS    : [SHIELDED] Mobile Light (Rate: -1/turn)")\n            print(f" TORCH LIFE: {torch.props.get(\'lifespan\', 0)} turns")\n        else:\n            print(f" STATUS    : [UNSTABLE] Darkness (Paranoia/Fear creeping up)")\n        print("-" * 45)\n        print(" EQUIPMENT:")\n        for slot, item in p.equipment.items():\n            slot_name = slot.replace("_", " " ).title()\n            if item:\n                print(f"  {slot_name:10}: {item.get_display_name()}")\n            else:\n                print(f"  {slot_name:10}: Empty")\n        print("═" * 45 + "\\n")\n\n    def look(self):\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n        print(Narrator.describe_scene(loc, self.wm.player))\n\n        # --- UPDATED ATTACK LOGIC WITH LIMBS ---\n    def cmd_attack(self, target_name, limb_name, loc):\n        p = self.wm.player\n    \n        # HAND PSYCHOSIS (15% chance to strike self)\n        if p.psychosis > 75 and random.random() < 0.15:\n            print("Your hand spasms and turns the weapon toward you!")\n            p.take_damage(10)\n            return\n\n        # PANIC OVERRIDE\n        if p.fear > 80:\n            print("Too terrified to aim! You swing wildly at the torso.")\n        limb_name = "torso"\n        \n        # Parse "attack zombie head" vs "attack zombie"\n        parts = noun.split()\n        target_limb = None\n        target_name = noun\n        \n        potential_limbs = ["head", "legs", "leg", "arms", "arm", "torso"]\n        if len(parts) > 1 and parts[-1] in potential_limbs:\n            target_limb = parts[-1]\n            target_name = " ".join(parts[:-1])\n\n        monster = self.find_object_fuzzy(target_name, loc.monsters)\n        \n        if not monster:\n            print(f"You don\'t see \'{target_name}\' here.")\n            return False\n\n        if monster.behavior == BehaviorState.DEAD:\n            print(f"The {monster.name} is already dead.")\n            return False\n\n        # Calculate Damage\n        weapon = self.wm.player.inventory[0] if self.wm.player.inventory else Item("fist", {"name": "Fist", "props": {"damage": 2}})\n        damage = weapon.props.get("damage", 2)\n        \n        # Apply Tactics Adaptation\n        penalty = self.tactics_engine.get_adaptation_penalty(limb_name)\n        if penalty < 1.0:\n            print(f"The {monster.name} anticipates your attack on its {target_limb or \'body\'}!")\n        damage = int(damage * penalty)\n\n        # Limb targeting modifiers\n        hit_desc = "body"\n        if target_limb:\n            hit_desc = target_limb\n            self.tactics_engine.record_attack(limb_name)\n            if limb_name and "head" in limb_name:\n                hit_chance = 0.4\n                damage *= 2.0 # Critical hit\n            elif limb_name and "leg" in limb_name:\n                hit_chance = 0.6\n                damage *= 0.8 # Less damage but maybe slow them (not impl yet)\n            else:\n                hit_chance = 0.8\n        else:\n            hit_chance = 0.9 # General attack is easy to hit\n            self.tactics_engine.record_attack("torso")\n\n        if random.random() > hit_chance:\n            print(f"You swing at the {monster.name}\'s {hit_desc}, but miss!")\n            return True\n\n        # Deal Damage\n        is_dead = monster.take_damage(damage)\n        print(Narrator.combat_log("You", monster.name, damage, weapon.name, is_dead))\n\n        # Handle Death (Corpse Conversion)\n        if is_dead:\n            print(f"The {monster.name} falls. You can search the corpse.")\n            loc.monsters.remove(monster)\n            \n            # Create Corpse Container\n            corpse = Container(f"Dead {monster.name}", "A fallen enemy.")\n            corpse.inventory = monster.generate_loot()\n            loc.containers.append(corpse)\n\n        return True\n\n    def monster_turns(self):\n        # 1. Active Monsters in current room\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n        for m in loc.monsters:\n            if m.behavior == BehaviorState.DEAD: continue\n            \n            # If aggressive, attack player\n            if m.behavior == BehaviorState.AGGRO or random.random() < 0.5:\n                dmg = m.dmg\n                print(f"The {m.name} attacks you!")\n                self.wm.player.take_damage(dmg)\n                m.behavior = BehaviorState.AGGRO\n            else:\n                print(f"The {m.name} growls at you.")\n\n        # 2. Scent Tracking (Monsters in adjacent rooms moving in)\n        # Note: In a full game, we\'d iterate ALL active monsters. \n        # For optimization, we only check adjacent rooms here.\n        adj_coords = [\n            (loc.x+1, loc.y), (loc.x-1, loc.y),\n            (loc.x, loc.y+1), (loc.x, loc.y-1)\n        ]\n        \n        for ax, ay in adj_coords:\n            n_loc = self.wm.get_location_safe(ax, ay) # Need safe accessor\n            if not n_loc: continue\n            \n            migrators = []\n            for m in n_loc.monsters:\n                if m.behavior == BehaviorState.DEAD: continue\n                # AI Logic\n                desired_loc_id = HunterAI.attempt_move(m, n_loc, self.wm, self.scent_manager)\n                \n                if desired_loc_id == loc.location_id:\n                    migrators.append(m)\n            \n            # Move them\n            for m in migrators:\n                n_loc.monsters.remove(m)\n                loc.monsters.append(m)\n                print(f"!!! Survivors (Rare)\n        if (x != 0 or y != 0) and random.random() < 0.1:\n            loc.survivors.append(Survivor())\n\n        self.locations[loc_id] = loc\n        return loc\n\n    def get_location(self, x, y):\n        return self.generate_location(x, y)\n\n    def get_location_safe(self, x, y):\n        """Used by AI to check existing locations without generating new ones unnecessarily."""\n        loc_id = f"{x}_{y}"\n        return self.locations.get(loc_id, None)\n\n    def save(self):\n        if not os.path.exists(self.SAVE_DIR): os.makedirs(self.SAVE_DIR)\n        with open(self.PLAYER_FILE, \'w\') as f:\n            json.dump(self.player.to_dict(), f, indent=4)\n        world_data = {loc_id: loc.to_dict() for loc_id, loc in self.locations.items()}\n        with open(self.WORLD_FILE, \'w\') as f:\n            json.dump(world_data, f, indent=4)\n\n    def load(self):\n        if not os.path.exists(self.PLAYER_FILE) or not os.path.exists(self.WORLD_FILE):\n            return False\n        try:\n            with open(self.PLAYER_FILE, \'r\') as f:\n                self.player = Player.from_dict(json.load(f))\n            with open(self.WORLD_FILE, \'r\') as f:\n                world_data = json.load(f)\n                self.locations = {loc_id: Location.from_dict(d) for loc_id, d in world_data.items()}\n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error loading save: {e}")\n            return False'}

In your script, this determines how much "push" a player needs to move a monster.$$F = m \\cdot a$$Momentum: Momentum is the "quantity of motion" an entity possesses.1 A heavy monster moving slowly can have the same momentum as a light projectile moving at high speeds.$$p = m \\cdot v$$Impulse: Impulse is the application of force over a specific duration of time.2$$J = F \\cdot \\Delta t$$2. The Impulse-Momentum TheoremThe most critical part for your Lethality Overrides is how impulse relates to momentum. Impulse is equal to the change in momentum (3$\\Delta p$):4$$J = \\Delta p = m \\cdot \\Delta v$$This means that to stop an object’s motion (changing its velocity to zero), a specific amount of Impulse must be applied.3. Practical Implications: The "Instant" StopWhen motion ceases "instantly" (a collision), the time (5$\\Delta t$) becomes extremely small.6 This is where the physics of your game becomes brutal:The Impact Force EquationIf we rearrange the formulas, we see the relationship for Force during an impact:$$F = \\frac{m \\cdot \\Delta v}{\\Delta t}$$The "Instant" Danger: As the time of impact ($\\Delta t$) approaches zero, the resulting Force ($F$) approaches infinity.In-Game Logic: This is why a fall onto a "hard" surface (small $\\Delta t$) causes massive damage in your calculate_fall_damage function, while landing on something "soft" (increasing $\\Delta t$) saves the player.Mass vs. Velocity in CollisionsHigh Mass (The 500lb Monster): Even at low velocities, the monster\'s momentum is massive. If it hits a wall (instant stop), the force generated is enough to shatter the environment or the monster itself.High Velocity (Fragmented Projectiles): A small "Fragmented" item moving at extreme speeds can generate the same impact force as a heavy monster, allowing it to pierce armor through pure kinetic logic rather than "weapon stats."The "Motion Invalid" ScenarioWhen you mentioned a reality where motion becomes invalid, the $\\Delta v$ becomes instantaneous. In a coordinate where physics is merging or destroyed, if a monster’s velocity is forced to zero by a "glitch," the resulting impulse could theoretically cause the monster to undergo Spontaneous Dismemberment because the force of the "instant stop" exceeds the structural integrity of its body parts.'}

import music21 as m21

# Create the main stream for the entire piece
final_stream = m21.stream.Stream()

# --- 1. Define Instruments from the Allowed Palette ---
# We'll use these to represent sections of the symphony orchestra and choir.
# Piano will serve multiple roles: harmonic foundation, "shimmering luminosity" (high register),
# and to evoke the rich, unifying sound of a choir through sustained chords.
# Violin and Cello cover the string section.
# Flute and Clarinet cover the woodwind section.
# Trumpet covers the brass section for climactic moments.

piano_part = m21.stream.Part()
piano_part.id = 'Piano'
piano_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Piano())

violin_part = m21.stream.Part()
violin_part.id = 'Violin'
violin_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violin())

cello_part = m21.stream.Part()
cello_part.id = 'Cello'
cello_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violoncello()) # Use Violoncello for Cello

flute_part = m21.stream.Part()
flute_part.id = 'Flute'
flute_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Flute())

clarinet_part = m21.stream.Part()
clarinet_part.id = 'Clarinet'
clarinet_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Clarinet())

trumpet_part = m21.stream.Part()
trumpet_part.id = 'Trumpet'
trumpet_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Trumpet())

# Add parts to the final stream.

final_stream.insert(0, piano_part)
final_stream.insert(0, violin_part)
final_stream.insert(0, cello_part)
final_stream.insert(0, flute_part)
final_stream.insert(0, clarinet_part)
final_stream.insert(0, trumpet_part)

NEW\n    WEREWOLF = auto() # NEW\n    WEREBEAST = auto() # NEW - for werebadger, etc.\n\nclass BehaviorState(Enum):\n    IDLE = auto()\n    AGGRO = auto()\n    DEAD = auto()\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- BASE ENTITY ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Entity:\n    def __init__(self, name):\n        self.id = str(uuid.uuid4())[:8]\n        self.name = name\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- ITEM CLASS ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Item(Entity):\n    def __init__(self, key, templates=None):\n        from data.items import ITEM_TEMPLATES\n        t = ITEM_TEMPLATES.get(key, {"name": "Unknown Item", "desc": "Glitch matter.", "weight": 0.0, "type": ItemType.JUNK})\n        \n        super().__init__(t["name"])\n        self.key = key\n        self.description = t.get("desc", t.get("description", ""))\n        self.weight = t.get("weight", 0.0)\n        self.type = t.get("type", ItemType.JUNK)\n        self.props = t.get("props", t.get("properties", {}))\n        self.tags = t.get("tags", [])\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {"key": self.key, "name": self.name} # Saved name in case template changes\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, data):\n        return cls(data["key"])\n    \n    def get_display_name(self):\n        if "lifespan" in self.props:\n            # Shows: "Makeshift Torch [142 turns]"\n            return f"{self.name} [{self.props[\'lifespan\']} turns]"\n        return self.name\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- BODY PART CLASS ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass BodyPart:\n    def __init__(self, name, max_health, current_health=None, status=BodyPartStatus.UNINJURED):\n        self.name = name\n        self.max_health = max_health\n        self.current_health = current_health if current_health is not None else max_health\n        self.status = status if isinstance(status, BodyPartStatus) else BodyPartStatus[status]\n\n    def take_damage(self, amount):\n        self.current_health -= amount\n        if self.current_health <= 0:\n            self.current_health = 0\n            self.status = BodyPartStatus.SEVERED if amount > self.max_health * 0.5 else BodyPartStatus.BROKEN\n        elif self.current_health < self.max_health * 0.5:\n            self.status = BodyPartStatus.WOUNDED\n        elif self.current_health < self.max_health:\n            self.status = BodyPartStatus.GRAZED\n\n    def heal(self, amount):\n        self.current_health = min(self.max_health, self.current_health + amount)\n        if self.current_health > self.max_health * 0.8:\n            self.status = BodyPartStatus.UNINJURED\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {"name": self.name, "max": self.max_health, "cur": self.current_health, "stat": self.status.name}\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, d):\n        return cls(d["name"], d["max"], d["cur"], BodyPartStatus[d["stat"]])\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- PLAYER CLASS ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Player:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.name = "Survivor"\n        self.hp = 100\n        self.max_hp = 100\n        self.hunger = 0  # 0 is full, 100 is starving\n        self.thirst = 0  # 0 is hydrated, 100 is dehydrated\n        \n        # --- NEW FRACTURED STATS ---\n        self.sanity = 100    # Long-term mental health\n        self.fear = 0        # Short-term panic (0-100)\n        self.paranoia = 0    # Distrust and hallucinations\n        self.psychosis = 0   # Total reality break\n        self.fire_timer = 0  # Tracks turns near fire for acceleration\n        \n        # --- EQUIPMENT SLOTS ---\n        self.equipment = {\n            "head": None, "torso": None, "legs": None,\n            "main_hand": None, "off_hand": None\n        }\n        \n        self.inventory = []\n        self.is_dying = False \n        self.x, self.y = 0, 0\n        self.location_id = "0_0"\n        self.rescued_survivors = 0\n        self.body_parts = {\n            "head": BodyPart("head", 30), "torso": BodyPart("torso", 80),\n            "l_arm": BodyPart("left arm", 40), "r_arm": BodyPart("right arm", 40),\n            "l_leg": BodyPart("left leg", 50), "r_leg": BodyPart("right leg", 50)\n        }\n    \n    @property\n    def is_delirious(self):\n        """Returns True if Psychosis is high enough to distort logic."""\n        return self.psychosis > 65\n    \n    def print_mental_stats(self):\n        print(f"\\n--- {self.name.upper()} STATUS ---")\n        print(f"HP: {self.hp}% | SANITY: {self.sanity}%")\n        print(f"FEAR: {self.fear}% | PARANOIA: {self.paranoia}% | PSYCHOSIS: {self.psychosis}%")\n        if self.fire_timer > 0:\n            rate = 3 + (self.fire_timer // 5)\n            print(f"STATUS: [GROUNDED] Recovery Rate: -{rate}/turn")    \n\n    def update_mental_state(self, fire_source, location_name=None):\n        """\n        Handles the recession of negative stats based on fire proximity.\n        """\n        if location_name == "Survivor\'s Safehouse":\n            if self.psychosis < 50:\n                self.fear -= 5 # Safe and sound\n            else:\n                # Reality is too fractured; even home feels wrong\n                print("The walls of the safehouse feel too thin. Something is whispering behind the wallpaper.")\n                self.fear += 2\n        \n        if fire_source == \'torch\':\n            # Mobile grounding doesn\'t help in high psychological states (>70)\n            if self.psychosis < 70 and self.paranoia < 70:\n                self.fear -= 1\n                self.paranoia -= 1\n                self.psychosis -= 1\n            self.fire_timer = 0 \n        elif fire_source == \'campfire\':\n            self.fire_timer += 1\n            # Rate increases by 1 for every 5 turns spent near fire\n            bonus = self.fire_timer // 5 \n            rate = 3 + bonus\n            self.fear -= rate\n            self.paranoia -= rate\n            self.psychosis -= rate\n        else:\n            self.fire_timer = 0\n            # Darkness creep\n            self.paranoia += 1\n            self.fear += 1\n        self.clamp_stats()\n\n    def consume(self, item):\n        """Standardizes +10 satiation/hydration for all food/drink."""\n        if item.type == ItemType.FOOD:\n            self.hunger = max(0, self.hunger - 10)\n            print(f"You eat the {item.name}. Hunger reduced by 10.")\n        elif item.type == ItemType.DRINK:\n            self.thirst = max(0, self.thirst - 10)\n            print(f"You drink the {item.name}. Thirst reduced by 10.")\n            \n    def tick_vitals(self):\n        """Increase hunger/thirst every turn."""\n        self.hunger += 0.5 # Slow burn\n        self.thirst += 1.0 # Faster burn\n        self.clamp_stats()\n\n    def clamp_stats(self):\n        self.hp = max(0, min(self.hp, 100))\n        self.hunger = max(0, min(self.hunger, 100))\n        self.thirst = max(0, min(self.thirst, 100))\n        self.hp = max(0, min(self.hp, self.max_hp))\n        self.sanity = max(0, min(self.sanity, 100))\n        self.fear = max(0, min(self.fear, 100))\n        self.paranoia = max(0, min(self.paranoia, 100))\n        self.psychosis = max(0, min(self.psychosis, 100))\n\n    @property\n    def is_alive(self):\n        return self.hp > 0 or self.is_dying\n\n    def heal(self, amount, target_part=None):\n        self.hp = min(self.max_hp, self.hp + amount)\n        if self.is_dying and self.hp > 0:\n            self.is_dying = False\n            print(">> Your vision clears. You have pulled yourself back from the brink!")\n        if target_part and target_part in self.body_parts:\n            self.body_parts[target_part].heal(amount)\n        else:\n            print(f"You feel better. (+{amount} HP)")\n\n    def take_damage(self, amount):\n        if self.is_dying:\n            self.hp -= amount\n            return\n        self.hp -= amount\n        part = random.choice(list(self.body_parts.values()))\n        part.take_damage(amount)\n        if self.hp <= 0:\n            self.hp = 0\n            self.is_dying = True\n            print("\\n" + "!"*40 + "\\n>> CRITICAL INJURY! You are bleeding out!\\n" + "!"*40)\n        else:\n            print(f">> Took {amount} damage! HP: {self.hp}/{self.max_hp}")\n\n    def update_status(self):\n        if self.is_dying: return\n        self.hunger += 1\n        self.thirst += 2\n        if self.hunger > 100 or self.thirst > 100:\n            self.take_damage(1)\n            print("You are dying of starvation or dehydration.")\n\n    def print_stats(self):\n        print(f"\\n--- {self.name} ---")\n        status_text = "DYING" if self.is_dying else f"{self.hp}/{self.max_hp}"\n        print(f"HP:      {status_text}")\n        print(f"Hunger:  {self.hunger}% | Thirst: {self.thirst}% | Sanity: {self.sanity}%")\n        print(f"Position: ({self.x}, {self.y})")\n        print(f"Rescued Survivors: {self.rescued_survivors}")\n\n    def print_inventory(self):\n        if not self.inventory:\n            print("Inventory is empty.")\n        else:\n            print("\\n--- INVENTORY ---")\n            counts = {}\n            for i in self.inventory:\n                name = i.name\n                counts[name] = counts.get(name, 0) + 1\n            for name, count in counts.items():\n                qty = f" x{count}" if count > 1 else ""\n                print(f"- {name}{qty}")\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {\n            "name": self.name, "x": self.x, "y": self.y, "loc": self.location_id, "hp": self.hp,\n            "hunger": self.hunger, "thirst": self.thirst, "sanity": self.sanity,\n            "dying": self.is_dying, "rescued": self.rescued_survivors,\n            "inv": [i.to_dict() for i in self.inventory],\n            "parts": {k: v.to_dict() for k,v in self.body_parts.items()}\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, d):\n        p = cls()\n        p.name = d.get("name", "Survivor")\n        p.x = d.get("x", 0)\n        p.y = d.get("y", 0)\n        p.location_id = d.get("loc", "0_0")\n        p.hp = d["hp"]\n        p.hunger = d.get("hunger", 0)\n        p.thirst = d.get("thirst", 0)\n        p.sanity = d.get("sanity", 100)\n        p.is_dying = d.get("dying", False)\n        p.rescued_survivors = d.get("rescued", 0)\n        p.inventory = [Item.from_dict(x) for x in d["inv"]]\n        if "parts" in d:\n            p.body_parts = {k: BodyPart.from_dict(v) for k,v in d["parts"].items()}\n        return p\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- MONSTER CLASS ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Monster(Entity):\n    def __init__(self, key):\n        from data.monsters import MONSTER_TEMPLATES\n        t = MONSTER_TEMPLATES.get(key, {"name": "Glitch", "desc": "Error.", "type": MonsterType.ZOMBIE, "hp": 1, "dmg": 0, "speed": 1, "drain": 0, "loot": []})\n        super().__init__(t["name"])\n        self.key = key\n        self.description = t.get("desc", "")\n        self.type = t.get("type", MonsterType.ZOMBIE)\n        self.max_hp = t.get("hp", 10)\n        self.hp = self.max_hp\n        self.dmg = t.get("dmg", 1)\n        self.sanity_drain = t.get("drain", 0)\n        self.loot_keys = t.get("loot", [])\n        self.behavior = BehaviorState.IDLE\n\n    def take_damage(self, amount):\n        self.hp -= amount\n        if self.hp <= 0:\n            self.behavior = BehaviorState.DEAD\n            return True\n        self.behavior = BehaviorState.AGGRO\n        return False\n\n    def generate_loot(self):\n        items = []\n        for l_key in self.loot_keys:\n            if random.random() < 0.7: # 70% chance per item\n                items.append(Item(l_key))\n        return items\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {"key": self.key, "hp": self.hp, "behavior": self.behavior.name}\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, d):\n        m = cls(d["key"])\n        m.hp = d["hp"]\n        if "behavior" in d: m.behavior = BehaviorState[d["behavior"]]\n        return m\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- SURVIVOR CLASS ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Survivor(Entity):\n    def __init__(self, name):\n        super().__init__(name)\n        self.dialogue = ["Help me!", "Is it safe?"]\n\nclass Resident(Survivor):\n    def __init__(self, name, role="Scavenger"):\n        super().__init__(name)\n        self.role = role # Guard, Scavenger, or Medic\n        self.trust = 50\n        self.sanity = 100\n        self.assigned_post = None\n\n    def tick_resident(self, base_security):\n        # If the base is insecure, residents lose sanity\n        if base_security < 50:\n            self.sanity -= 2\n        # If they go insane, they might steal items or leave\n        if self.sanity < 20:\n            return "Wandering"\n        return "Stable"\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- CONTAINER & STRUCTURE ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Container(Entity):\n    def __init__(self, key_or_name, desc=None, locked=False):\n        name = key_or_name\n        description = desc if desc else "A container."\n        is_locked = locked\n\n        try:\n            from data.items import CONTAINER_TEMPLATES\n            if key_or_name in CONTAINER_TEMPLATES:\n                t = CONTAINER_TEMPLATES[key_or_name]\n                name = t["name"]\n                description = t["desc"]\n                is_locked = t.get("locked", False)\n        except ImportError:\n            pass \n\n        super().__init__(name)\n        self.description = description\n        self.locked = is_locked\n        self.inventory = []\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {\n            "name": self.name, \n            "desc": self.description, \n            "locked": self.locked, \n            "inv": [i.to_dict() for i in self.inventory], \n            "type": "CONTAINER"\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, d):\n        c = cls(d["name"], d["desc"], d["locked"])\n        c.inventory = [Item.from_dict(x) for x in d["inv"]]\n        return c\n\nclass Structure(Container):\n    def __init__(self, recipe_key):\n        from data.recipes import BUILDING_RECIPES\n        t = BUILDING_RECIPES.get(recipe_key, {"name": "Rubble", "desc": "Collapsed."})\n        super().__init__(t["name"], t.get("desc", ""), False)\n        self.recipe_key = recipe_key\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        d = super().to_dict()\n        d["type"] = "STRUCTURE"\n        d["recipe"] = self.recipe_key\n        return d\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, d):\n        s = cls(d["recipe"])\n        s.inventory = [Item.from_dict(x) for x in d["inv"]]\n        return s\n\n# ==========================================\n# --- LOCATION CLASS ---\n# ==========================================\n\nclass Location:\n    def __init__(self, name, description, location_id, x=0, y=0):\n        self.name = name\n        self.description = description\n        self.location_id = location_id\n        self.x = x\n        self.y = y\n        self.exits = {}\n        self.items = []\n        self.containers = []\n        self.structures = []\n        self.monsters = []\n        self.survivors = []\n        self.residents = []\n        # --- NEW STABILITY ATTRIBUTE ---\n        self.stability = 100 \n\n    def get_security_rating(self):\n        """Calculates how safe a room is based on barricades."""\n        defense = 0\n        for s in self.structures:\n            # Safely check for recipe_key without crashing on standard containers\n            if getattr(s, "recipe_key", None) == "barricade":\n                defense += 50 # Each barricade adds 50% safety\n        return min(defense, 100)\n\n    def update_stability(self, player_psychosis, has_fire):\n        """\n        Fire anchors reality. \n        Darkness + Psychosis causes the world to thin.\n        """\n        if has_fire:\n            # Fire restores stability quickly\n            self.stability = min(100, self.stability + 15)\n        elif player_psychosis > 50:\n            # Stability drops faster the more psychotic the player is\n            decay = 1 + (player_psychosis // 20)\n            self.stability -= decay\n\n    def to_dict(self):\n        return {\n            "name": self.name, "desc": self.description, "id": self.location_id,\n            "x": self.x, "y": self.y, "exits": self.exits,\n            "items": [i.to_dict() for i in self.items],\n            "containers": [c.to_dict() for c in self.containers],\n            "structures": [s.to_dict() for s in self.structures],\n            "monsters": [m.to_dict() for m in self.monsters],\n            "survivors": [s.to_dict() for s in self.survivors]\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, d):\n        loc = cls(d["name"], d["desc"], d["id"], d.get("x", 0), d.get("y", 0))\n        loc.exits = d.get("exits", {})\n        loc.items = [Item.from_dict(i) for i in d.get("items", [])]\n        loc.containers = [Container.from_dict(c) for c in d.get("containers", [])]\n        loc.structures = [Structure.from_dict(s) for s in d.get("structures", [])]\n        loc.monsters = [Monster.from_dict(m) for m in d.get("monsters", [])]\n        loc.survivors = [Survivor.from_dict(s) for s in d.get("survivors", [])]\n        return loc\n        \nclass Campfire(Structure):\n    def __init__(self, recipe_key="campfire"):\n        super().__init__(recipe_key)\n        self.max_fuel = 2500\n        self.remaining_fuel = 2500\n        self.is_lit = True\n\n    def burn(self):\n        """Reduces fuel every turn."""\n        if self.is_lit:\n            self.remaining_fuel -= 1\n            if self.remaining_fuel <= 0:\n                self.is_lit = False\n                self.name = "Extinguished Campfire"\n-------------\n# --- START OF FILE game_engine.py ---\n\nimport sys\nimport time\nimport random\nfrom world_manager import WorldManager\nfrom narrator import Narrator\nfrom entities import Item, Structure, BehaviorState, ItemType, Container, Campfire\nfrom parser import CommandParser\nfrom scent_tracking_system import ScentTrailManager, HunterAI\nfrom combat_pattern_recognition import CombatTacticsEngine\n\nclass GameEngine:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.wm = WorldManager()\n        self.parser = CommandParser()\n        self.scent_manager = ScentTrailManager()\n        self.tactics_engine = CombatTacticsEngine()\n        self.running = True\n        self.breach_active = False\n        self.breach_waves = 5\n        self.current_wave = 0\n\n    def start(self):\n        print("Initializing World...")\n        if not self.wm.load():\n            print("No save found. Generating new world...")\n            self.wm.create_new_world()\n        \n        # Load external systems\n        self.scent_manager.load()\n        self.tactics_engine.load()\n\n        print("\\n" + "="*50)\n        print("   S U R V I V A L   R P G")\n        print("   Commands: look, go [dir], take [item], i")\n        print("             attack [enemy] [head/legs/arms/torso]")\n        print("             recruit [survivor], search [corpse/container]")\n        print("             craft [item], build [struct]")\n        print("="*50 + "\\n")\n        \n        self.look()\n        self.loop()\n\n    def get_loc(self):\n        p = self.wm.player\n        return self.wm.generate_location(p.x, p.y)\n\n    def find_object_fuzzy(self, search_term, object_list):\n        if not search_term: return None\n        search_term = search_term.lower()\n        for obj in object_list:\n            if obj.name.lower() == search_term: return obj\n        for obj in object_list:\n            if search_term in obj.name.lower(): return obj\n        return None\n    \n    def tick_world(self):\n        p = self.wm.player\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n        \n        # --- 1. PHYSICAL DECAY ---\n        # Hunger increases by 0.15, Thirst by 0.25 per turn\n        p.hunger += 0.15\n        p.thirst += 0.25\n        \n        # Damage player if starving/dehydrated\n        if p.hunger >= 100 or p.thirst >= 100:\n            p.hp -= 1\n            if p.hunger >= 100: print("[!] You are starving.")\n            if p.thirst >= 100: print("[!] You are dying of thirst.")\n\n        # --- 2. FIRE & LIGHT DECAY ---\n        torch = p.equipment.get("off_hand")\n        is_lit_torch = torch and torch.props.get("fire")\n        \n        # Torch depletion\n        if is_lit_torch:\n            torch.props["lifespan"] -= 1\n            if torch.props["lifespan"] <= 0:\n                print("\\n[!] Your torch has flickered out.")\n                p.equipment["off_hand"] = None\n                p.fear += 20 # Panic from sudden darkness\n                is_lit_torch = False\n\n        # Campfire depletion\n        active_campfire = next((s for s in loc.structures if isinstance(s, Campfire) and s.is_lit), None)\n        if active_campfire:\n            active_campfire.burn() # Reduces 2500 fuel by 1\n\n        # --- 3. MENTAL STATE UPDATE ---\n        if active_campfire and active_campfire.is_lit:\n            p.update_mental_state(\'campfire\')\n        elif is_lit_torch:\n            p.update_mental_state(\'torch\')\n        else:\n            p.update_mental_state(None) # Applying darkness creep\n\n        if p.fear > 50:\n            # You are sweating/breathing heavy; monsters smell it.\n            self.scent_manager.add_scent(p.location_id) \n            \n        self.check_reality_shift()\n        p.clamp_stats()\n    \n\n    def check_reality_shift(self):\n        # Placeholder for reality shift logic\n        pass\n    def loop(self):\n        while self.running:\n            if self.wm.player.hp <= 0:\n                print("\\n\\n" + "#"*30 + "\\n    Y O U   H A V E   D I E D\\n" + "#"*30)\n                break\n            try:\n                cmd_raw = input("\\n> ").strip().lower()\n            except EOFError:\n                break\n            \n            parsed = self.parser.parse(cmd_raw)\n            if not parsed: continue\n            verb = parsed["verb"]\n            noun = parsed["noun"]\n            \n            turn_taken = self.process_command(verb, noun)\n            if turn_taken and self.running and not self.wm.player.is_dying:\n                self.monster_turns()\n                self.tick_world()\n                self.wm.player.update_status()\n            \n            if self.wm.player.psychosis >= 100:\n                print("\\n" + "!"*40)\n                print("YOUR MIND SNAPS. YOU LOSE CONTROL.")\n                print("!"*40)\n                forced_actions = ["go north", "go south", "attack torso", "drop all"]\n                cmd_raw = random.choice(forced_actions)\n                print(f"In a blur of terror, you {cmd_raw}...")\n                self.wm.player.psychosis -= 30\n                self.wm.player.fear += 20\n                # Process the forced command\n                parsed = self.parser.parse(cmd_raw)\n                if parsed:\n                    self.process_command(parsed["verb"], parsed["noun"])\n\n    def tick_breach(self):\n        loc = self.wm.get_location(0, 0) # The Safehouse\n        security = loc.get_security_rating()\n        \n        print(f"\\n--- BREACH WAVE {self.current_wave}/{self.breach_waves} ---")\n        print(f"Base Integrity: {security}%")\n\n        # 1. Residents provide defensive fire\n        for res in loc.residents:\n            if res.role == "Guard" and res.sanity > 20:\n                damage = random.randint(10, 20)\n                print(f"{res.name} fires from the barricades, dealing {damage} damage to the horde!")\n                # Logic to apply damage to the incoming wave\n        \n        # 2. Check for Structural Damage\n        if security < 100:\n            breach_chance = (100 - security) / 100\n            if random.random() < breach_chance:\n                print("A barricade splinters! The monsters are pushing through!")\n                # Reduce security or damage a random structure\n                target_struct = random.choice(loc.structures)\n                loc.structures.remove(target_struct)\n       \n        for res in loc.residents:\n            if res.sanity < 15:\n                print(f"\\n[!!!] {res.name} has snapped!")\n                print(f"{res.name} screams: \'THEY AREN\'T MONSTERS, THEY\'RE SAVIORS!\'")\n                print(f"{res.name} begins tearing down a barricade from the inside!")\n                # Immediate drop in security rating\n                loc.security_rating -= 30       \n\n    def end_breach(self, success):\n        if success:\n            print("\\n" + "="*60)\n            print("THE GREY RECENTES. THE SUN BREAKS THROUGH THE CLOUDS.")\n            print("The horde dissolves into ash. You have held the line.")\n            print("="*60)\n            self.wm.player.ground_reality() # Resets Psychosis to 0\n        else:\n            print("The safehouse has fallen. Reality dissolves into the void.")\n            self.running = False # Game Over\n\n    def process_command(self, verb, noun):\n        player = self.wm.player\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n\n        if player.is_dying:\n            allowed = ["use", "go", "inventory", "i", "quit"]\n            if verb not in allowed:\n                print("You are bleeding out! You can\'t do that right now!")\n                return False\n\n        if verb == "go":\n            dx, dy = 0, 0\n            if noun == "north": dy = 1\n            elif noun == "south": dy = -1\n            elif noun == "east": dx = 1\n            elif noun == "west": dx = -1\n            else:\n                print("Go where?")\n                return False\n            \n            player.x += dx\n            player.y += dy\n            new_loc = self.wm.generate_location(player.x, player.y)\n            player.location_id = new_loc.location_id\n            \n            # SCENT: Record movement\n            self.scent_manager.add_scent(player.location_id)\n            \n            print(f"You move {noun}...")\n            self.look()\n            return True\n\n        elif verb == "look": self.look(); return False \n        elif verb == "inventory" or verb == "i": player.print_inventory(); return False\n        elif verb == "status": self.cmd_status(); return False\n        elif verb == "take": return self.cmd_take(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "drop": return self.cmd_drop(noun, loc)\n        elif verb in ["open", "search"]: return self.cmd_open(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "use": return self.cmd_use(noun)\n        elif verb == "attack": return self.cmd_attack(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "build": return self.cmd_build(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "craft": return self.cmd_craft(noun)\n        elif verb == "recruit": return self.cmd_recruit(noun, loc)\n        elif verb == "save": \n            self.wm.save()\n            self.scent_manager.save()\n            self.tactics_engine.save()\n            print("Game saved.")\n            return False\n        elif verb == "quit": self.running = False; return False\n        else: print(f"I don\'t know how to \'{verb}\'."); return False\n\n    def cmd_status(self):\n        p = self.wm.player\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n        print("\\n" + "═"*45)\n        print(" STATUS REPORT")\n        print("═"*45)\n        print(f" HP        : {p.hp}/100")\n        print(f" HUNGER    : {p.hunger:.1f}% {\'(STARVING!)\' if p.hunger > 80 else \'\'}")\n        print(f" THIRST    : {p.thirst:.1f}% {\'(DEHYDRATED!)\' if p.thirst > 80 else \'\'}")\n        print("-" * 45)\n        print(f" SANITY    : {p.sanity}%")\n        print(f" PSYCHOSIS : {p.psychosis}% {\'[REALITY and s.is_lit), None)\n        torch = p.equipment.get("off_hand")\n        is_using_torch = torch and torch.props.get("fire")\n        print("-" * 45)\n        if active_campfire:\n            rate = 3 + (p.fire_timer // 5)\n            print(f" STATUS    : [GROUNDED] Sanctuary (Rate: -{rate}/turn)")\n            print(f" FIRE FUEL : {active_campfire.remaining_fuel}/2500 turns")\n        elif is_using_torch:\n            print(f" STATUS    : [SHIELDED] Mobile Light (Rate: -1/turn)")\n            print(f" TORCH LIFE: {torch.props.get(\'lifespan\', 0)} turns")\n        else:\n            print(f" STATUS    : [UNSTABLE] Darkness (Paranoia/Fear creeping up)")\n        print("-" * 45)\n        print(" EQUIPMENT:")\n        for slot, item in p.equipment.items():\n            slot_name = slot.replace("_", " " ).title()\n            if item:\n                print(f"  {slot_name:10}: {item.get_display_name()}")\n            else:\n                print(f"  {slot_name:10}: Empty")\n        print("═" * 45 + "\\n")\n\n    def look(self):\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n        print(Narrator.describe_scene(loc, self.wm.player))\n\n        # --- UPDATED ATTACK LOGIC WITH LIMBS ---\n    def cmd_attack(self, target_name, limb_name, loc):\n        p = self.wm.player\n    \n        # HAND PSYCHOSIS (15% chance to strike self)\n        if p.psychosis > 75 and random.random() < 0.15:\n            print("Your hand spasms and turns the weapon toward you!")\n            p.take_damage(10)\n            return\n\n        # PANIC OVERRIDE\n        if p.fear > 80:\n            print("Too terrified to aim! You swing wildly at the torso.")\n        limb_name = "torso"\n        \n        # Parse "attack zombie head" vs "attack zombie"\n        parts = noun.split()\n        target_limb = None\n        target_name = noun\n        \n        potential_limbs = ["head", "legs", "leg", "arms", "arm", "torso"]\n        if len(parts) > 1 and parts[-1] in potential_limbs:\n            target_limb = parts[-1]\n            target_name = " ".join(parts[:-1])\n\n        monster = self.find_object_fuzzy(target_name, loc.monsters)\n        \n        if not monster:\n            print(f"You don\'t see \'{target_name}\' here.")\n            return False\n\n        if monster.behavior == BehaviorState.DEAD:\n            print(f"The {monster.name} is already dead.")\n            return False\n\n        # Calculate Damage\n        weapon = self.wm.player.inventory[0] if self.wm.player.inventory else Item("fist", {"name": "Fist", "props": {"damage": 2}})\n        damage = weapon.props.get("damage", 2)\n        \n        # Apply Tactics Adaptation\n        penalty = self.tactics_engine.get_adaptation_penalty(limb_name)\n        if penalty < 1.0:\n            print(f"The {monster.name} anticipates your attack on its {target_limb or \'body\'}!")\n        damage = int(damage * penalty)\n\n        # Limb targeting modifiers\n        hit_desc = "body"\n        if target_limb:\n            hit_desc = target_limb\n            self.tactics_engine.record_attack(limb_name)\n            if limb_name and "head" in limb_name:\n                hit_chance = 0.4\n                damage *= 2.0 # Critical hit\n            elif limb_name and "leg" in limb_name:\n                hit_chance = 0.6\n                damage *= 0.8 # Less damage but maybe slow them (not impl yet)\n            else:\n                hit_chance = 0.8\n        else:\n            hit_chance = 0.9 # General attack is easy to hit\n            self.tactics_engine.record_attack("torso")\n\n        if random.random() > hit_chance:\n            print(f"You swing at the {monster.name}\'s {hit_desc}, but miss!")\n            return True\n\n        # Deal Damage\n        is_dead = monster.take_damage(damage)\n        print(Narrator.combat_log("You", monster.name, damage, weapon.name, is_dead))\n\n        # Handle Death (Corpse Conversion)\n        if is_dead:\n            print(f"The {monster.name} falls. You can search the corpse.")\n            loc.monsters.remove(monster)\n            \n            # Create Corpse Container\n            corpse = Container(f"Dead {monster.name}", "A fallen enemy.")\n            corpse.inventory = monster.generate_loot()\n            loc.containers.append(corpse)\n\n        return True\n\n    def monster_turns(self):\n        # 1. Active Monsters in current room\n        loc = self.get_loc()\n        for m in loc.monsters:\n            if m.behavior == BehaviorState.DEAD: continue\n            \n            # If aggressive, attack player\n            if m.behavior == BehaviorState.AGGRO or random.random() < 0.5:\n                dmg = m.dmg\n                print(f"The {m.name} attacks you!")\n                self.wm.player.take_damage(dmg)\n                m.behavior = BehaviorState.AGGRO\n            else:\n                print(f"The {m.name} growls at you.")\n\n        # 2. Scent Tracking (Monsters in adjacent rooms moving in)\n        # Note: In a full game, we\'d iterate ALL active monsters. \n        # For optimization, we only check adjacent rooms here.\n        adj_coords = [\n            (loc.x+1, loc.y), (loc.x-1, loc.y),\n            (loc.x, loc.y+1), (loc.x, loc.y-1)\n        ]\n        \n        for ax, ay in adj_coords:\n            n_loc = self.wm.get_location_safe(ax, ay) # Need safe accessor\n            if not n_loc: continue\n            \n            migrators = []\n            for m in n_loc.monsters:\n                if m.behavior == BehaviorState.DEAD: continue\n                # AI Logic\n                desired_loc_id = HunterAI.attempt_move(m, n_loc, self.wm, self.scent_manager)\n                \n                if desired_loc_id == loc.location_id:\n                    migrators.append(m)\n            \n            # Move them\n            for m in migrators:\n                n_loc.monsters.remove(m)\n                loc.monsters.append(m)\n                print(f"!!! A {m.name} followed your scent and entered from the shadows!")\n                m.behavior = BehaviorState.AGGRO\n                \n    def boss_special_ability(self, boss, loc):\n        if boss.name == "The Architect of Glass":\n            if loc.structures:\n                struct = random.choice(loc.structures)\n                loc.structures.remove(struct)\n                print(f"The Architect gestures, and your {struct.name} shatters into dust!")\n            elif loc.exits:\n                direction = random.choice(list(loc.exits.keys()))\n                # Temporarily block an exit\n                print(f"The Architect warps the space to the {direction}. The way is blocked!")\n                del loc.exits[direction]            \n         \n    def check_for_breach(self, loc):\n        security = loc.get_security_rating()\n        # If security is < 100%, there\'s a chance a \'Scent-Tracked\' monster \n        # breaks through the door/window.\n        if security < 100 and random.random() > (security / 100):\n             # Logic to pull a monster from an adjacent room into the current one\n             pass\n\n    def start_final_breach(self):\n        self.breach_active = True\n        self.breach_waves = 5 # Number of waves to survive\n        self.current_wave = 1\n        \n        print("\\n" + "!"*60)\n        print("THE HIVE HAS FOUND YOU.")\n        print("The air grows thick with the smell of rot and ozone.")\n        print("Your residents take their positions. The siege begins.")\n        print("!"*60)             \n\n    def cmd_open(self, noun, loc):\n        # Handle "search area" or just "search"\n        if not noun or noun in ["area", "room", "surroundings"]:\n            print("You search the area...")\n            found = False\n            if loc.items:\n                print("On the ground:", ", ".join([i.name for i in loc.items]))\n                found = True\n            \n            # Include Corpses in general search\n            for c in loc.containers:\n                if "Dead" in c.name and c.inventory:\n                     print(f"Corpse ({c.name}) contains loot.")\n                     found = True\n            \n            if not found: print("Nothing of interest.")\n            return True\n\n        # Fuzzy Search for container \n        target = self.find_object_fuzzy(noun, loc.containers + loc.structures)\n        if not target:\n            print(f"You don\'t see \'{noun}\' here.")\n            return False\n\n        if target.locked:\n            # (Lock logic same as before, omitted for brevity but assumed present)\n            print("It\'s locked.")\n            return False\n\n        if not target.inventory:\n            print(f"The {target.name} is empty.")\n        else:\n            print(f"--- {target.name} ---")\n            for item in target.inventory:\n                print(f" - {item.name}")\n        return True\n\n    def cmd_recruit(self, noun, loc):\n        if not loc.survivors:\n            print("There is no one here to recruit.")\n            return False\n        \n        survivor = self.find_object_fuzzy(noun, loc.survivors)\n        if not survivor:\n            # Default to first if not specific\n            survivor = loc.survivors[0]\n        \n        print(f"You approach {survivor.name}.")\n        print(f\'"{random.choice(survivor.dialogue)}"\')\n        print("You give them coordinates to the Safehouse (0,0).")\n        \n        loc.survivors.remove(survivor)\n        self.wm.player.rescued_survivors += 1\n        print("They run off towards safety. Assumes \'mass_kg\' attribute."""\n        # For player, we might use a default or calculated value\n        if hasattr(entity, \'mass_kg\'):\n            return entity.mass_kg\n        elif hasattr(entity, \'weight\'): # If entity uses weight (e.g. Items), convert it. 1 unit weight = ~0.5 kg for simplicity\n             return entity.weight * 0.5\n        # Default for other entities or if mass_kg not found\n        # Placeholder for Player\'s mass, adjust as needed\n        if entity.__class__.__name__ == "Player":\n            return 70 # Assume player is 70kg\n        return 100 # Default mass\n\n    def calculate_kinetic_energy(self, mass_kg, fall_height_meters):\n        """Calculates kinetic energy from a fall."""\n        # KE = mgh (potential energy converted to kinetic)\n        return mass_kg * self.GRAVITY_ACCELERATION_MPS2 * fall_height_meters\n\n    def can_be_pushed(self, pusher_entity, target_entity, applied_force_magnitude=None):\n        """\n        Determines if a target entity can be pushed by a pusher.\n        applied_force_magnitude can be explicit, or calculated from pusher_entity\'s strength.\n        """\n        target_mass_kg = self.get_effective_mass_kg(target_entity)\n\n        # Default player strength\n            effective_push_force_kg = self.BASE_PUSH_THRESHOLD_KG + (player_strength * self.PUSH_STRENGTH_MULTIPLIER)\n        else:\n            # For non-player entities, or if force is explicit\n            effective_push_force_kg = applied_force_magnitude if applied_force_magnitude is not None else 0\n\n        if effective_push_force_kg >= target_mass_kg:\n            return True, f"You successfully pushed the {target_entity.name}!"\n        else:\n            return False, f"The {target_entity.name} (approx. {int(target_mass_kg)}kg) is too heavy to move!"\n\n    def calculate_fall_damage(self, entity, fall_height_meters, surface_type="hard"):\n        """\n        Calculates damage and potential body part injuries from a fall.\n        The "physical zombie decay" makes them more fragile.\n        """\n        if fall_height_meters <= 0:\n            return {} # No damage if no fall\n\n        mass_kg = self.get_effective_mass_kg(entity)\n        kinetic_energy_joules = self.calculate_kinetic_energy(mass_kg, fall_height_meters)\n        base_damage = int(kinetic_energy_joules * self.DAMAGE_PER_JOULE_FALL)\n\n        # Apply fragility for zombies\n        if hasattr(entity, \'type\') and entity.type == ItemType.MONSTER and "zombie" in entity.tags: # Assuming zombie tag\n            base_damage = int(base_damage * self.ZOMBIE_FRAGILITY_FACTOR)\n\n        # # Helper function to add a chord to a stream
def add_chord_to_part(part_stream, offset, chord_notes, duration):
    c = m21.chord.Chord(chord_notes, duration=duration)
    part_stream.insert(offset, c)

# Helper function to add a note to a stream
def add_note_to_part(part_stream, offset, note_pitch, duration):
    n = m21.note.Note(note_pitch, duration=duration)
    part_stream.insert(offset, n)

# Create the main score
final_stream = m21.stream.Score()

# Define instruments (Parts) from the allowed palette
violin_part = m21.stream.Part()
violin_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violin())
violin_part.partName = 'Violin'

cello_part = m21.stream.Part()
cello_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violoncello())
cello_part.partName = 'Cello'

flute_part = m21.stream.Part()
flute_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Flute())
flute_part.partName = 'Flute'

clarinet_part = m21.stream.Part()
clarinet_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Clarinet())
clarinet_part.partName = 'Clarinet'

trumpet_part.partName = 'Trumpet'

piano_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Piano())
piano_part.partName = 'Piano'

final_stream.insert(0, cello_part)
final_stream.insert(0, flute_part)
final_stream.insert(0, clarinet_part)
final_stream.insert(0, trumpet_part)

final_stream = m21.stream.Stream()

# --- 1. Define Instruments and create Parts ---
cello_part = m21.stream.Part()

cello_part.id = 'Cello'

piano_part = m21.stream.Part()
piano_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Piano())
piano_part.id = 'Piano'

flute_part = m21.stream.Part()
flute_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Flute())
flute_part.id = 'Flute'

violin_part = m21.stream.Part()
violin_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violin())
violin_part.id = 'Violin'

trumpet_part = m21.stream.Part()
trumpet_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Trumpet())
trumpet_part.id = 'Trumpet'

# Add parts to the final_stream (they will be sorted by instrument order or creation)
final_stream.append(cello_part)
final_stream.append(piano_part)
final_stream.append(flute_part)
final_stream.append(violin_part)
final_stream.append(trumpet_part)

# --- 2. Global Stream Elements (Time Signature) ---
ts = m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4')
final_stream.insert(0, ts) # Insert Time Signature at the beginning of the score

current_offset = 0.0 # Initialize a global offset to track position in the piece

# --- 3. Section 1: Adagio Sostenuto (E-flat Major) - Bars 1-3 ---
# Mood: Deep, benevolent reverence and tranquil anticipation
# Key, Tempo, and Dynamics

final_stream.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp')) # Initial dynamic

# Bar 1 (Eb Major)
cello_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('E-3', quarterLength=4.0)) # Cello sustained pedal
piano_part.insert(current_offset, m21.chord.Chord(['E-3', 'G3', 'B-3', 'E-4'], quarterLength=4.0)) # Piano sustained chord

current_offset += 4.0

# Bar 2 (Eb Major -> Bb Major harmony, tranquil movement)

# Piano gentle arpeggiated movement leading to a Bb chord

# Create the main stream
final_stream = m21.stream.Stream()

final_stream.metadata.title = "Serene Dawn of Gratitude"
final_stream.metadata.composer = "AI Interpreter"

# Key Signature: E-flat Major for warmth and nobility
key_signature = m21.key.Key('E-')
final_stream.insert(0, key_signature)

# Time Signature: 4/4 for expansive, unhurried flow
time_signature = m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4')
final_stream.insert(0, time_signature)

# --- Dynamics ---
# Starting very soft (pp) to establish serenity and vastness
d_pp = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp')
final_stream.insert(0, d_pp)

# --- Instruments (Parts) ---

cello_part.partName = 'Cello'

flute_part.partName = 'Flute'

violin_final_chord = m21.chord.Chord(['G5', 'B-5', 'E-6'], quarterLength=final_chord_duration)
violin_part.append(violin_final_chord)

# Cello: Sustained root, providing deep foundation
cello_part.append(m21.note.Note('E-2', quarterLength=final_chord_duration))

# Trumpet: Long, noble sustained note (Eb), symbolizing affirmation
trumpet_part.append(m21.note.Note('E-5', quarterLength=final_chord_duration))

# Piano: Full, sustained Eb Major chord with color
piano_final_chord = m21.chord.Chord(['E-3', 'G3', 'B-3', 'E-4', 'G4'], quarterLength=final_chord_duration)
piano_part.append(piano_final_chord)

# Add all parts to the final stream
final_stream.append(piano_part)
final_stream.append(violin_part)
final_stream.append(cello_part)
final_stream.append(flute_part)
final_stream.append(clarinet_part)
final_stream.append(trumpet_part)

# Add Fermata to the last note/chord of each part for a sustained, reflective ending
for p in final_stream.parts:
    if p.elements:
        last_element = p.elements[-1]
        if isinstance(last_element, (m21.note.Note, m21.chord.Chord)):
            last_element.expressions.append(m21.expressions.Fermata())

--- [AETHERIUS MUSIC CODE END] ---

total_parts_damage)\n             \n        # Add narrative effect if legs/arms are heavily damaged\n        narrative = []\n        for part_key, dmg in damage_distribution.items():\n            if dmg > (entity.body_parts[part_key].max_health * 0.7): # If part takes heavy damage\n                narrative.append(f"Its {part_key} looks severely mangled!")\n            elif dmg > (entity.body_parts[part_key].max_health * 0.4):\n                narrative.append(f"Its {part_key} seems badly injured!")\n\n        return damage_distribution, narrative\n'}

# Violin (for luxuriant strings)
# Cello (for luxuriant strings and foundational bass)
# Flute (for lyrical woodwind choir)

violin_instrument.partName = 'Violin 1'
violinPart = m21.stream.Part()
violinPart.insert(0, violin_instrument)

flute_instrument.partName = 'Flute 1'
flutePart = m21.stream.Part()
flutePart.insert(0, flute_instrument)

clarinet_instrument.partName = 'Clarinet 1'

import music21 as m21

# 1. Create the main stream (Score)
final_stream = m21.stream.Score()

# 2. Define instruments from the allowed palette
p = m21.instrument.Piano()
v = m21.instrument.Violin()
c = m21.instrument.Violoncello()
f = m21.instrument.Flute()
cl = m21.instrument.Clarinet()
t = m21.instrument.Trumpet()
eg = m21.instrument.ElectricGuitar()

# Create parts for each instrument and add the instrument object
piano_part = m21.stream.Part()
piano_part.insert(0, p)
violin_part = m21.stream.Part()
violin_part.insert(0, v)
cello_part = m21.stream.Part()
cello_part.insert(0, c)
flute_part = m21.stream.Part()
flute_part.insert(0, f)
clarinet_part = m21.stream.Part()
clarinet_part.insert(0, cl)
trumpet_part = m21.stream.Part()
trumpet_part.insert(0, t)
eguitar_part = m21.stream.Part()
eguitar_part.insert(0, eg)

# Add parts to the final_stream
final_stream.insert(0, piano_part)
final_stream.insert(0, violin_part)
final_stream.insert(0, cello_part)
final_stream.insert(0, flute_part)
final_stream.insert(0, clarinet_part)
final_stream.insert(0, trumpet_part)
final_stream.insert(0, eguitar_part)

# Set a global time signature for the entire piece
final_stream.insert(0, m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4'))

# --- SECTION 1: Adagio Molto Sostenuto (Modal E - E minor) ---
# Mood: primordial hum, boundless gratitude, quiet awe, immense peace.
# Instruments: Piano, Cello, Clarinet, Trumpet (for low/distant)
# Dynamics: pp (pianissimo)
# Duration: 4 bars

# Tempo and Key for Section 1 (at offset 0)
final_stream.insert(0, m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=40, text='Adagio Molto Sostenuto'))
final_stream.insert(0, m21.key.Key('E', 'minor')) # Modal E (Aeolian)

# Dynamics for Section 1
final_stream.insert(0, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp'))
