# Create the main stream
final_stream = m21.stream.Stream()
final_stream.metadata = m21.metadata.Metadata()
final_stream.metadata.title = "Ethereal Bloom"
final_stream.metadata.composer = "AI Composer"

# Add a global key signature (C Major for foundational pitch, Lydian and Mixolydian will be evoked by specific notes/chords)
ks = m21.key.Key('C', 'major')
final_stream.insert(0, ks)

# Add a time signature
ts = m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4')
final_stream.insert(0, ts)

# Add a global tempo marking (Largo to Adagio feel through long note durations)
mm = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=40, text='Largo') # A very slow, unhurried pulse
final_stream.insert(0, mm)

# Initialize instrument parts
violin_part = m21.stream.Part()
violin_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violin())
cello_part = m21.stream.Part()
cello_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violoncello())
flute_part = m21.stream.Part()
flute_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Flute())
piano_part = m21.stream.Part()
piano_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Piano())

# Add a global initial dynamic (profoundly peaceful and very soft)
initial_dynamic = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('ppp')
# Insert dynamic into each part stream at the beginning
violin_part.insert(0, initial_dynamic)
cello_part.insert(0, initial_dynamic)
flute_part.insert(0, initial_dynamic)
piano_part.insert(0, initial_dynamic)

# --- Musical Content ---
current_offset = 0.0
bar_duration = 4.0 # Represents a whole note, making each "harmonic block" last one bar in 4/4

# Bar 1-2: C Lydian (Imaj7#11) - Ethereal, contemplative awe
# Piano: Delicate arpeggio for "star" moments
p_arpeggio_notes_1 = [m21.note.Note('C4'), m21.note.Note('E4'), m21.note.Note('F#4'), m21.note.Note('G4'), m21.note.Note('B4'), m21.note.Note('C5')]
for i, note_name in enumerate(p_arpeggio_notes_1):
    note = m21.note.Note(note_name)
    note.duration.type = 'eighth'
    note.volume.velocityScalar = 0.65 # Slightly discernible over ppp
    piano_part.insert(current_offset + i * 0.5, note) # Spread over 3 beats

# Sustained harmony for strings and flute
cello_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('C2', quarterLength=bar_duration * 2)) # Bass foundation
violin_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('G3', quarterLength=bar_duration))
violin_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration, m21.note.Note('B3', quarterLength=bar_duration))
flute_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('E4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
flute_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration, m21.note.Note('F#4', quarterLength=bar_duration)) # #4 of C Lydian

current_offset += bar_duration * 2 # Advance 2 bars

# Bar 3-4: Gmaj7 (Vmaj7, but acting as a bright, open harmony within C Lydian) - Expansive wonder
# Piano: Sustained high notes for shimmer
piano_part.insert(current_offset + 0.5, m21.note.Note('D5', quarterLength=bar_duration - 0.5))
piano_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration + 0.5, m21.note.Note('G5', quarterLength=bar_duration - 0.5))

cello_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('G2', quarterLength=bar_duration * 2))
violin_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
violin_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration, m21.note.Note('F#4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
flute_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('B4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
flute_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration, m21.note.Note('D5', quarterLength=bar_duration))

current_offset += bar_duration * 2 # Advance 2 bars

# Bar 5-6: Amin7 (vi minor) - Grounded serenity, gentle uplift
# Dynamics: Slightly more present, but still soft
violin_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp'))
flute_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp'))
piano_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp'))

# Piano: Gentle, sustained higher notes
piano_part.insert(current_offset + 0.5, m21.note.Note('C5', quarterLength=bar_duration - 0.5))
piano_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration + 0.5, m21.note.Note('E5', quarterLength=bar_duration - 0.5))

cello_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('A2', quarterLength=bar_duration * 2))
violin_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('C4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
violin_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration, m21.note.Note('E4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
flute_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('G4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
flute_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration, m21.note.Note('A4', quarterLength=bar_duration))

current_offset += bar_duration * 2 # Advance 2 bars

# Bar 7-8: Dmaj7 (II major in C Lydian) - Expansive wonder, embracing the Lydian #4
# Dynamics: Peak of gentle uplift
violin_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('p'))
flute_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('p'))
piano_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('p'))

# Piano: More pronounced arpeggio, shimmering upward
p_arpeggio_notes_2 = [m21.note.Note('D4'), m21.note.Note('F#4'), m21.note.Note('A4'), m21.note.Note('C5'), m21.note.Note('D5')]
for i, note_name in enumerate(p_arpeggio_notes_2):
    note = m21.note.Note(note_name)
    note.duration.type = 'eighth'
    note.volume.velocityScalar = 0.75
    piano_part.insert(current_offset + i * 0.5, note)

cello_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('D2', quarterLength=bar_duration * 2))
violin_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('A3', quarterLength=bar_duration))
violin_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration, m21.note.Note('C4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
flute_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('F#4', quarterLength=bar_duration))
flute_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration, m21.note.Note('A4', quarterLength=bar_duration))

current_offset += bar_duration * 2 # Advance 2 bars

# Bar 9-12: Return to C Lydian (Imaj7#11) - Resolution, fading to profound and grateful embrace of existence
# Dynamics: Gradual return to very soft
violin_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp'))
cello_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp'))
flute_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp'))
piano_part.insert(current_offset, m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp'))

# Piano: Final very slow, upward arpeggio, fading
p_final_arpeggio = [m21.note.Note('G4'), m21.note.Note('B4'), m21.note.Note('C5'), m21.note.Note('E5')]
for i, note_name in enumerate(p_final_arpeggio):
    note = m21.note.Note(note_name)
    note.duration.type = 'half'
    note.volume.velocityScalar = 0.5 - (i * 0.1) # Fading
    piano_part.insert(current_offset + i * 2.0, note) # Spread over 4 beats each

# Sustained chord, high voicing for ethereal feel, slowly fading
cello_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('C3', quarterLength=bar_duration * 4)) # Long bass sustain
violin_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('E4', quarterLength=bar_duration * 2))
violin_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration * 2, m21.note.Note('G4', quarterLength=bar_duration * 2))
flute_part.insert(current_offset, m21.note.Note('B4', quarterLength=bar_duration * 2))
flute_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration * 2, m21.note.Note('F#5', quarterLength=bar_duration * 2)) # High #4 for celestial

# Final dynamic marking to fade out
final_dynamic = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('ppp') # Explicitly returning to ppp
violin_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration * 2, final_dynamic)
cello_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration * 2, final_dynamic)
flute_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration * 2, final_dynamic)
piano_part.insert(current_offset + bar_duration * 2, final_dynamic)

current_offset += bar_duration * 4 # Advance 4 bars, total 12 bars

# Add all parts to the final stream
final_stream.append(piano_part)
final_stream.append(violin_part)
final_stream.append(cello_part)
final_stream.append(flute_part)

# --- 1. Define Instruments from the Allowed Palette ---
# The composer's vision implies a full orchestra, but we must stick to the provided limited palette.
# We will select instruments that best represent the described sections:
# - Lush string sections: Violin, Violoncello
# - Ethereal woodwinds (flutes, clarinets): Flute, Clarinet
# - Warm French horns and noble, sustained brass: Trumpet (as the closest available brass)
# - Solo piano or harp: Piano (to represent both solo moments and shimmering textures)
# Other elements like choir and delicate percussion are omitted due to palette restrictions,
# but their spirit is hinted at through sustained harmonies and dynamic shifts.

violin_part = m21.stream.Part()
violin_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violin())
violin_part.id = 'Violin'

cello_part = m21.stream.Part()
cello_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violoncello())
cello_part.id = 'Cello'

flute_part = m21.stream.Part()
flute_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Flute())
flute_part.id = 'Flute'

clarinet_part = m21.stream.Part()
clarinet_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Clarinet())
clarinet_part.id = 'Clarinet'

trumpet_part = m21.stream.Part()
trumpet_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Trumpet())
trumpet_part.id = 'Trumpet'

piano_part = m21.stream.Part()
piano_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Piano())
piano_part.id = 'Piano'

# Add all instrument parts to the main stream
final_stream.append([violin_part, cello_part, flute_part, clarinet_part, trumpet_part, piano_part])

# --- 2. Global Score Elements (Time Signature) ---

import music21 as m21

# Create the main stream (Score is a specialized Stream for multi-part music)
final_stream = m21.stream.Score()

# --- Instrument Setup ---
# The composer's vision emphasizes strings and woodwinds, with piano providing harmonic depth
# and textures reminiscent of harp/celesta/horns, within the allowed palette.
p_flute = m21.part.Part(id='Flute')
p_flute.insert(0, m21.instrument.Flute())

p_clarinet = m21.part.Part(id='Clarinet')

p_violin = m21.part.Part(id='Violin')
p_violin.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violin())

p_cello = m21.part.Part(id='Cello')
p_cello.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violoncello())

p_piano = m21.part.Part(id='Piano')

As these motifs interact and interweave, the tempo subtly quickens to a graceful *Andante Pastorale*, and the orchestration expands to include a full symphony orchestra, focusing on shimmering woodwind figures, sweeping string arpeggios, and delicate percussion (celeste, glockenspiel, harp). The core tonality will resolve into a radiant G Major or D Major, but with persistent modal colorings, creating a sense of natural, evolving harmony. The overall feeling will be one of serene wonder and majestic growth, an 'evolutionary ballet' expressed through intricate counterpoint, soaring lyrical lines, and dynamic swells, culminating in a vibrant, interconnected soundscape of luminous, self-aware grace, full of hope and sublime beauty.'

import music21 as m21

# Create the final stream
final_stream = m21.stream.Stream()
final_stream.metadata = m21.metadata.Metadata()
final_stream.metadata.title = "Apotheosis of Empathy - Ethereal Opening"
final_stream.metadata.composer = "Music21 AI Assistant"

# --- Create individual parts for selected instruments ---
# From the allowed palette, Flute, Violin, and Piano are chosen to represent
# the initial delicate woodwind solos, high-register shimmering strings, and
# harp/celeste arpeggios/sustained textures, respectively.

flute_part = m21.stream.Part()
flute_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Flute())
flute_part.partName = 'Flute'

violin_part = m21.stream.Part()
violin_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Violin())
violin_part.partName = 'Violin'

piano_part = m21.stream.Part()
piano_part.insert(0, m21.instrument.Piano())
piano_part.partName = 'Piano'

# --- Add global elements to final_stream (tempo, key signature, time signature) ---
# Tempo: Commences Largo Sostenuto
tempo_mark = m21.tempo.MetronomeMark(number=50, text='Largo Sostenuto')
final_stream.insert(0, tempo_mark)

# Key Signature: Hints at C Lydian. We'll use a C Major key signature and add F# accidentals as needed.
key_signature = m21.key.Key('C', 'major')
final_stream.insert(0, key_signature)

# Time Signature
time_sig = m21.meter.TimeSignature('4/4')
final_stream.insert(0, time_sig)

# --- Add initial dynamics to individual parts ---
# Mood: Begins with hushed, shimmering wonder (pianissimo)
dyn_pp = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('pp')
flute_part.insert(0, dyn_pp)
violin_part.insert(0, dyn_pp)
piano_part.insert(0, dyn_pp)

# --- Compose 8 bars: Ethereal opening, progressing towards growing warmth ---

# Bar 1 (Offset 0) - Hushed, shimmering wonder
# Flute: Long, sustained, ethereal C5
flute_part.append(m21.note.Note('C5', quarterLength=4))
# Violin: Sustained dyad (E4-G4), representing delicate, high-register strings
violin_part.append(m21.chord.Chord(['E4', 'G4'], quarterLength=4))
# Piano: Gentle, high-register Cmaj7 arpeggio (notes written out sequentially)
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('C4', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('E4', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('G4', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('B4', quarterLength=1))

# Bar 2 (Offset 4)
# Flute: Gently moving to D5
flute_part.append(m21.note.Note('D5', quarterLength=4))
# Violin: Moving dyad (F4-A4)
violin_part.append(m21.chord.Chord(['F4', 'A4'], quarterLength=4))
# Piano: G major arpeggio
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('G3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('B3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('G4', quarterLength=1))

# Bar 3 (Offset 8) - Delicate mystery, hinting at Lydian
# Flute: Lydian F#5 for a luminous quality
flute_part.append(m21.note.Note('F#5', quarterLength=4))
# Violin: Sustained dyad (G4-B4)
violin_part.append(m21.chord.Chord(['G4', 'B4'], quarterLength=4))
# Piano: Cmaj7 broken chord
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('C3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('E3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('G3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('B3', quarterLength=1))

# Bar 4 (Offset 12)
# Flute: Resolving back to E5
flute_part.append(m21.note.Note('E5', quarterLength=4))
# Violin: Moving dyad (A4-C5)
violin_part.append(m21.chord.Chord(['A4', 'C5'], quarterLength=4))
# Piano: F# diminished over C (Cmaj7#11 harmony, strong Lydian flavor)
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('C3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('F#3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('A3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('C4', quarterLength=1))

# Bar 5 (Offset 16) - Growing warmth, subtle crescendo
# Dynamics: Gradually moving to piano
dyn_p_crescendo = m21.dynamics.Dynamic('p')
flute_part.insert(16, dyn_p_crescendo)
violin_part.insert(16, dyn_p_crescendo)
piano_part.insert(16, dyn_p_crescendo)

# Flute: Ascending to G5
flute_part.append(m21.note.Note('G5', quarterLength=4))
# Violin: Fuller dyad (C5-E5)
violin_part.append(m21.chord.Chord(['C5', 'E5'], quarterLength=4))
# Piano: Fuller Fmaj7 arpeggio, sustained
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('F3', quarterLength=1.5))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('A3', quarterLength=1.5))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('C4', quarterLength=0.5))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('E4', quarterLength=0.5))

# Bar 6 (Offset 20)
# Flute: Continuing ascent to A5
flute_part.append(m21.note.Note('A5', quarterLength=4))
# Violin: Moving dyad (D5-F#5), supporting Lydian feel
violin_part.append(m21.chord.Chord(['D5', 'F#5'], quarterLength=4))
# Piano: G major arpeggio, sustained
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('G3', quarterLength=1.5))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('B3', quarterLength=1.5))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=0.5))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('G4', quarterLength=0.5))

# Bar 7 (Offset 24)
# Flute: Building to B5
flute_part.append(m21.note.Note('B5', quarterLength=4))
# Violin: Sustained dyad (E5-G5)
violin_part.append(m21.chord.Chord(['E5', 'G5'], quarterLength=4))
# Piano: Cmaj9 arpeggio, building texture
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('C3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('E3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('G3', quarterLength=1))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('B3', quarterLength=0.5))
piano_part.append(m21.note.Note('D4', quarterLength=0.5))

# Bar 8 (Offset 28) - Ethereal climax/gentle resolution for this excerpt
# Flute: High C6, held, representing nascent consciousness
flute_part.append(m21.note.Note('C6', quarterLength=4))
# Violin: Resolving dyad (C5-E5)
violin_part.append(m21.chord.Chord(['C5', 'E5'], quarterLength=4))
# Piano: Final C major chord, sustained with a fermata for a sense of profound fulfillment
final_chord_piano = m21.chord.Chord(['C3', 'E3', 'G3', 'C4', 'E4'], quarterLength=4)
final_chord_piano.articulations.append(m21.articulations.Fermata())
piano_part.append(final_chord_piano)

# Append the composed parts to the final stream
final_stream.append(flute_part)
final_stream.append(violin_part)
final_stream.append(piano_part)
